#PROJECT
PR:PROJECT_TITLE                 	Metabolomic Profiling of the Malaria Box Reveals Antimalarial Target Pathways
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	Here we interrogated the in vitro metabolic effects of 189 drugs (including 169
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	of the drug-like compounds from the Malaria Box) using ultra-high performance
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	liquid chromatography mass-spectrometry (UHPLC-MS). The resulting metabolic
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	fingerprints provide information on the parasite biochemical pathways affected
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	by pharmacologic intervention and offer a critical blueprint for selecting and
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	advancing lead compounds as next-generation antimalarial drugs. Our results
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	reveal several major classes of metabolic disruption, which allow us to predict
PR:PROJECT_SUMMARY               	the mode-of-action (MoA) for many of the Malaria Box compounds.
PR:INSTITUTE                     	Penn State University
PR:LAST_NAME                     	Llinas
PR:FIRST_NAME                    	Manuel
PR:ADDRESS                       	W126 Millenium Science Complex, University Park, PA 16802
PR:EMAIL                         	manuel@psu.edu
PR:PHONE                         	(814) 867-3527
#STUDY
ST:STUDY_TITLE                   	Metabolomic Profiling of the Malaria Box Reveals Antimalarial Target Pathways
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	Here we interrogated the in vitro metabolic effects of 189 drugs (including 169
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	of the drug-like compounds from the Malaria Box) using ultra-high performance
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	liquid chromatography mass-spectrometry (UHPLC-MS). The resulting metabolic
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	fingerprints provide information on the parasite biochemical pathways affected
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	by pharmacologic intervention and offer a critical blueprint for selecting and
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	advancing lead compounds as next-generation antimalarial drugs. Our results
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	reveal several major classes of metabolic disruption, which allow us to predict
ST:STUDY_SUMMARY                 	the mode-of-action (MoA) for many of the Malaria Box compounds.

#COLLECTION
CO:COLLECTION_SUMMARY            	Cells were pelleted and the media aspirated prior to methanol extraction
#TREATMENT
TR:TREATMENT_SUMMARY             	Magnetically purified iRBCs (~20uL) were treated with >2XIC50 drug for 2.5 hours
#SAMPLEPREP
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	90% Methanol/10% water at 50:1 solvent/cell pellet followed by vortexing and
SP:SAMPLEPREP_SUMMARY            	clarification via centrifugation
SP:PROCESSING_METHOD             	Lysis
SP:PROCESSING_STORAGE_CONDITIONS 	4 C
SP:EXTRACT_CLEANUP               	Clarification via centrifugation followed by nitrogen drying
SP:EXTRACT_STORAGE               	-80 C
SP:SAMPLE_RESUSPENSION           	6X pellet volume of HPLC H2O
SP:SAMPLE_SPIKING                	Internal Standard 13C4, 15N1-Aspartate used for sample preparation normalizer

CH:CHROMATOGRAPHY_TYPE           	Reversed phase
